style="color:#b3b3b3;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:110%;padding-left:7.48pt">Our Board of Directors has authorized the repurchase in the future of an additional up to $250 million of our common stock</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#34;We are proud of our solid first quarter results which as expected, are down from our industry&#8217;s uniquely exceptional first quarter of 2021, but consistent with the new level of operating success Jefferies achieved for the last nine months of 2021.  Our strong first quarter results reflect the breadth and depth of our platform, despite the challenging trading environment caused by the anticipated change in Fed policy that existed in December and January and exacerbated by the even more difficult capital markets conditions that began in February with the onset of the invasion of Ukraine.  Despite the change in market tone, the performance in our Investment Banking business continues to reflect our increased market share, as continued momentum in our Advisory business led our results, with an increase of 75% over the prior year comparable quarter.  Our debt underwriting net revenues were solid, while our equity underwriting results were lower than the same period last year, consistent with a reduction in industry-wide deal activity.  The new issue markets are clearly more sensitive to the increase in volatility and while our investment banking backlog</font><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%;position:relative;top:-3.5pt;vertical-align:baseline">5</font><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%"> remains strong, our realization of this backlog is sensitive to market conditions.</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#34;Equities net revenues were impacted by market volatility and global instability.  Fixed Income net revenues were lower, primarily due to lower trading volumes in the face of inflation concerns and interest rate uncertainty.  </font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#34;Asset Management net revenues reflect higher asset management fees, offset by lower investment returns and lower revenues from strategic affiliates as compared to the prior year quarter.</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#8220;We have no operations in Russia and our exposure to Russia is otherwise immaterial.</font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">&#34;Our Ukrainian Doing Good Global Trading Day on March 3</font><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%;position:relative;top:-3.5pt;vertical-align:baseline">rd</font><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%"> raised more than $14 million, our largest fundraising effort ever.  We are humbled by our clients, employees, shareholders and friends who have all come together in this show of support.  The funds were distributed to 20 charities that are providing on the ground humanitarian aid and support to help the brave, courageous and inspirational people of Ukraine as they defend their lives, freedom and homes.  We hope and pray for their fortitude and success.  It should be crystal clear that Jefferies stands with the Ukrainian people.&#34; </font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:22.5pt"><font style="color:#0084bf;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:110%">Richard Handler, CEO, and Brian Friedman, President </font></div><div Refer to schedule on page 9 for reconciliation to U.S. GAAP amounts.</font></div><div style="text-indent:2.15pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:15.85pt;text-indent:-15.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%">2.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%;padding-left:7.93pt">Allocated net interest represents an allocation to Asset Management of certain of our long-term debt interest expense, net of interest income on our Cash and cash equivalents and other sources of liquidity.  Allocated net interest has been disaggregated to increase transparency and to make clearer actual Investment return.  Refer to Selected Financial and Statistical Information on pages 6 to 7.</font></div><div style="text-indent:2.15pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:15.85pt;text-indent:-15.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%">3.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%;padding-left:7.93pt">The 137.292 million common shares repurchased since January 2018 includes 133.449 million shares of common stock repurchased in the open market for $2.979 billion under our Board of Director authorizations and 3.843 million shares of common stock for $128.6 million repurchased in connection with net-share settlements under our equity compensation plan.</font></div><div style="text-indent:2.15pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:15.85pt;text-indent:-15.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%">4.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%;padding-left:7.93pt">Tangible shareholders' equity (a non-GAAP financial measure), is defined as Jefferies Financial Group shareholders' equity less Intangible assets, net and goodwill.  Refer to schedule on page 9 for reconciliation to U.S. GAAP amounts.</font></div><div style="text-indent:2.15pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:15.85pt;text-indent:-15.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%">5.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%;padding-left:7.93pt">Backlog represents an estimate of our net revenues from expected future transactions.  As an indicator of net revenues in a given future period, it is subject to limitations.  The time frame for the realization of revenues from these expected transactions varies and is influenced by factors we do not control.  Transactions not included in the estimate may occur, and expected transactions may also be modified or cancelled. </font></div><div style="text-indent:2.15pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:15.85pt;text-indent:-15.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%">6.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:105%;padding-left:7.93pt">In the first quarter of 2022, we transferred certain Merchant Banking net assets to our Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management segments. Previously reported results are presented on a comparable basis.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(3)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Allocated net interest is not separately disaggregated for Investment Banking and Capital Markets. This presentation is aligned to our Investment Banking and Capital Markets internal performance measurement.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(4)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Includes management and performance fees from funds and accounts managed by us as well as our share of fees received by affiliated asset management companies with which we have revenue and profit share arrangements, as well as earnings on our ownership interest in affiliated asset managers.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(5)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Allocated net interest represents an allocation to Asset Management of certain of our long-term debt interest expense, net of interest income on our Cash and cash equivalents and other sources of liquidity. Allocated net interest has been disaggregated to increase transparency and to make clearer actual Investment return. We believe that aggregating Investment return and Allocated net interest would obscure the Investment return by including an amount that is unique to our credit spreads, debt maturity profile, capital structure, liquidity risks and allocation methods.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(6)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Number of trading loss days is calculated based on trading activities in our Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management business segments.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(7)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">VaR estimates the potential loss in value of trading positions in our Investment Banking and Capital Markets and Asset Management business segments due to adverse market movements over a one-day time horizon with a 95% confidence level. For a further discussion of the calculation of VaR, see &#34;Value-at-Risk&#34; in Part II, Item 7A &#34;Quantitative and Qualitative Disclosures About Market Risk&#34; in our Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended November 30, 2021.</font></div><div style="height:44.36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><table style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(2)</font><font classified as such under Accounting Standards Codification 820, accounted for at fair value and included within Financial instruments owned.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(3)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Tangible equity (a non-GAAP financial measure) represents total Jefferies shareholders' equity less goodwill and identifiable intangible assets. We believe that tangible equity is meaningful for valuation purposes, as financial companies are often measured as a multiple of tangible equity, making these ratios meaningful for investors.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(4)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Leverage ratio equals total assets divided by total equity.</font></div><div style="margin-top:3pt;padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-27pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%">(5)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Roboto Light',sans-serif;font-size:9.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:125%;padding-left:15.63pt">Tangible gross leverage ratio (a non-GAAP financial measure) equals total assets less goodwill and identifiable intangible assets divided by tangible equity. The tangible gross leverage ratio is used by rating agencies in assessing our leverage ratio.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.05pt"><font><br></font></div><div
